#-------------------------------------------------------
# Stability script
#
# Version: 1.7
# Author: Dimitrios Simatos
# Last updated: 2021-12-28
#-------------------------------------------------------
# Description
#
# This script is designed to measure in static mode, when the flow cell is filled manually.
#-------------------------------------------------------
# Changes
#
#-------------------------------------------------------
# Important points
#
#-------------------------------------------------------
# Things to do before running the script
#
# Set time units to minutes.
# Set filenames.
#-------------------------------------------------------
# Pumping cycles and execution time
#
# There is only 1 step, with 360 cycles.
# Execution time: 720 x 2 = 1440 minutes = 24 hours
# There are 720 cycles, each one consisting of 2 minutes of measurements.
# The first cycle has the initialization command uncommented and the first report valve command commented.
#-------------------------------------------------------
# Volume of liquid needed
#
# Only enough liquid to fill the flow cell.
#-------------------------------------------------------
# SPA settings
itime l 0.04
gaterangemode l
drainrangemode l
#-------------------------------------------------------
# Cycle 1: Measuring for 2 minutes
filename step_1_up-H2O_initial_
transfer d 0 -1 -0.1 -1 -1 0
wait 15000 #wait 15 seconds
transfer d 0 -1 -0.1 -1 -1 0
wait 15000 #wait 15 seconds
transfer d 0 -1 -0.1 -1 -1 0
wait 15000 #wait 15 seconds
